Welcome to Tyrant route!

……何とも言いようがない。　現状では判断材料がいかにも不足だ。
...... I can't say enough about it.　In the current situation, how insufficient is the material for judgment.

六波羅に銃口を向けた以上、彼らの苛政に加担する者ではない。　そうは思うものの、そのＧＨＱの肩書きは、敵意はともかく警戒心を呼ぶには充分に足りていた。
As long as he had pointed the muzzle at Muhaara, he would not be a party to their tyranny.　Although he thought so, the title of GHQ was enough to call for caution, if not hostility.

しかし信用云々はさておいて、後々のことを考えるに、今この場で虚言を吐くことは厄介を招くだけとも思える。　正直に話しておくのが無難かもしれない。
However, trust aside, it seems to me that telling falsehoods here and now will only lead to trouble later on.　It might be safer to be honest.

「鎌倉警察署の湊斗景明です。　先程の行為は一身上の都合による振舞い、差し出た真似とお咎めなくば重畳。感謝などして頂くには及びません」
This is Minato Kageaki of the Kamakura Police Department.　What you just did was for your own personal reasons. There is no need for you to thank me.

「あら、あら。そんなご謙遜はなさらないで。　命を救っておきながら感謝はするななんて、それではわたくし、恩知らずの恥知らず者になるしかありませんもの。ねえ、ばあや？」
"Oh, my. Don't be so modest.　Don't be so modest. If you save my life but don't thank me, then I'll become an ungrateful and shameless person. Hey, Grandma?

"Yes. Yes, indeed.　 Minato-sama, even though I owe you a great debt of gratitude, I would appreciate it if you would refrain from humiliating your daughter by making her feel ungrateful and ashamed.

"I never intended it that way.　But I was rude. I apologize.

……なるほど。　確かに、彼女の立場から見ればそういう話か。
...... I see.　That's certainly the story from her perspective.

彼女に果たして助けが必要だったのか、その点には一抹の疑念があるとしても。あの時の彼女の振舞いを今にして思い返せば、竜騎兵を相手取っても何らかの方法で切り抜ける自信はあったように思える。
Even though I have some doubts about whether she really needed help or not. Looking back on her behavior at the time, she seemed confident that she could have gotten through the dragon craft soldiers in some way.

だがそうとしても、礼節を知る人間であれば、与えられた援助を無用と決め付けることに恥を覚えずにはいられまい。礼にて返すべし、その心情は理解が及ぶ。　心中で頷きながら、俺は頭を下げた。
But even so, a person who knows civility cannot help but feel ashamed of assuming that the help given is useless. You should return the favor with gratitude, and I understand that sentiment.　I nodded in my mind and bowed my head.

女性と老婦が顔を見合わせ、くすくすと笑う。　二人にすれば俺のこんな態度も可笑しいのだろうか。
The woman and the old woman looked at each other and chuckled.　I wonder if they find this attitude of mine funny.

――暴兵の手から村人の窮地を救っていたこの女性。　俺に言わせれば、彼女が俺に感謝すべき理由は本当に全く無いのだが、それは当人の知る由もない事だ。
--This woman who had been saving the villagers from the hands of the ruffians.　If you ask me, there's really no reason at all for her to be grateful to me, but that's something she has no way of knowing.

「あらいけない。申し遅れました。　ＧＨＱ民政局の、大鳥香奈枝です。恩人に先に名乗らせてしまって、こちらこそ無礼をお詫びしなくてはなりませんね」
"Oh, no. I'm sorry I'm late.　I'm Ootori Kanae of the Civil Affairs Bureau at GHQ. I must apologize for my rudeness in letting my benefactor identify himself first.

「あ、これはさよがうっかりしておりました。村長どのには既に挨拶を済ませていたもので……どうかお許しを、湊斗さま。　私めは香奈枝の侍従、永倉でございます」
"Oh, this is Sayo's mistake. I had already greeted the village chief. ...... Please forgive me, Minato-sama. I am Nagakura, attendant to Kanae.

Polite.　 Lieutenant Ootori-dono. Lord Commander Nagakura.

――未熟。　声なく、俺は呟いた。
--Inexperience.　I muttered to myself without a voice.

悔いるならば、最初から殺さねば良い。　殺したからには、悔いなど抱くべきではない。
If you regret it, you should not have killed him in the first place.　Once you have killed, you should not have any regrets.

もっと良い手段があったのでは、などと思うのなら最初からそうしていれば良い。　殺すほかなく殺したのなら、なぜ殺した後に迷いを抱こうか。
If you think you could have done something better, you should have done it from the beginning.　If I had no choice but to kill him, why would I have any doubts afterwards?

結局のところ、悔いなど、殺したという事実に耐えられない心が欲する慰めに過ぎないのだ。　その意味で、襲われたから仕方なかったのだと言い訳するのと何も変わらない。
In the end, regret is just a comfort that the mind that can't stand the fact that you killed someone needs.　In that sense, it is no different from making excuses that you had no choice because you were attacked.

殺さぬつもりで殺したのなら技量未熟。　殺すつもりで殺して悔いるのならば心術未熟。　　そう、胸中に断ずる。
If you kill with the intention of not killing, your skill is inexperienced.　If you killed with the intention of killing and regretted it, your mind is inexperienced.　　That's what I've decided in my heart.

……とはいえ。　そのようなこと、何もしなかった人間に言われる筋合いではないだろう。俺は手前勝手な感想を口にするのは控えた。
Even though .......　I'm sure you'll find a lot of people who've never done anything like this before. I refrained from giving my selfish opinion.

...... Enough. Spectator.

It's called "musha-style striking.

It was thanks to her that the boys accompanying me were safe at that time.　She refused to thank me, but now that we've met, I guess I should say it again.

考える間に、先方が口を開いていた。

That time I was on my knees, today I'm a spectator.　I'm impressed with the police these days.

露骨な挙措で唾を吐き捨てる少女、一条。　成程、そう思われるのは仕方ない事だった。物陰に隠れて黙って見ていれば普通、人は怯えて立ち竦んでいると考える。
The girl, Ichijou, spat at me in a blatant manner. Yes, I could not help but think that. If you hide in the shadows and watch in silence, people usually think you're cowering in fear.

実際、やっていることに変わりはなかったのだからどう思われようが文句を言える筋でもない。　人の危難を看過した者としては、謝罪が必要だろう。俺は神妙に頭を下げた。
In fact, there was no change in what he was doing, so he had no right to complain regardless of what people thought.　As someone who had overlooked the danger of others, I felt the need to apologize. I bowed my head curiously.

〝金翅鳥王剣〟
"Golden-winged Bird King Ken

マックス・インメルマン中尉。　外暦一九一四年から一九一八年にわたって戦われた欧州戦争において、比類なき勇名を鳴り響かせた独逸の誇る撃墜王の一人である。
Lieutenant Max Immelmann.　He was one of Germany's proudest shot-down kings who made a name for himself with his unparalleled bravery during the European War fought from 1914 to 1918.

その名に〝侯〟の一語が無い事からも明らかな通り、彼は竜騎兵団に属してはいたものの、騎士階級の出身ではなかった。　真打劔冑の継承者ではなかったのである。
Although he was a member of the Dragon Craft Corps, he was not from the crafting class, as evidenced by the absence of the word "lord" in his name.　He was not the heir to the "Shin-uchi tsurugi*".

この時代の撃墜王としては異例と云わねばならない。　外暦一九〇〇年代初頭（国紀二五〇〇年代中盤）はまだ数打劔冑が開発されて間もない頃であり、現在に比べれば性能は著しく低いレベルに留まっていた。
I must say that this is unusual for a downed king of this era.　In the early 1900's (mid 1950's), the tsurugi* had just been developed, and its performance was still remarkably low compared to today.

彼が愛騎としたフォッカーＥ３とてもそうだ。　張線支持を採用した単翼騎――当時代の技術の粋が凝らされた騎体ではあったが、真打劔冑との性能差を埋めるものでは到底ない。
The Fokker E3, which he considered his favorite craft, is no different.　It was a single-wing craft with taut-wire support - a craft body that incorporated the best of the technology of the time, but it was far from enough to make up for the difference in performance of the Tsurugi*-tono.

その頃、戦場に華を添えた各国の撃墜王――由緒正しい名門の騎士であり最高の劔冑を継承していた人々――と、一介の騎兵将校インメルマンとの間に、騎体性能の点で巨大な隔絶があったことは確実である。
It is certain that there was a huge gap in terms of craft performance between the shoot-down kings of various countries who added their splendor to the battlefield at that time - the venerable and prestigious craftmen who had inherited the highest tsurugi* - and Immelmann, a simple craft officer.

しかも、彼の配属された北フランス戦線は敵に正規の騎士が多く、対して味方の騎士は大半が対露戦線に派遣されていたためほとんど皆無という、実に苛酷を極める状況下にあった。
In addition, he was assigned to the Northern France front, where the enemy had many regular craftmen, while there were almost no friendly craftmen because most of them had been sent to the front against Russia.

味方は彼を含めて新弱の竜騎兵ばかり。　敵方は古強の騎士が居並ぶ。　……武功を掲げるどころか、生き残るだけでも至難であったに違いない。
He and his teammates are all new and weak dragon crafters.　I'm not sure what to make of it.　In the event that you've got a lot of time and energy, you'll be able to take advantage of it.

その死線にあってインメルマンを撃墜王たらしめたのは、少年期に出会った異国人との体験だった。
What made Immelmann the king of shooting down the enemy was an experience he had with a foreigner when he was a boy.

徳川時代の幕引き後、大和はやや閉鎖的であった前時代の反動のように西洋文化を多く取り入れ、何それとなく学んだが、軍事編制においてはプロイセン――ドイツに倣う所が非常に多かった。
After the end of the Tokugawa era, Yamato adopted a lot of Western culture as a reaction to the previous era, which had been somewhat closed off, and learned more than a few things.

プロイセン軍こそ欧州最精強と見る向きが強かったためである。　幾度となく軍事交流団が派遣され、貪欲に技術知識を求めた。
This was because the Prussian army was considered by many to be the strongest in Europe.　The Prussian army was seen by many as the most powerful in Europe, and military exchange delegations were dispatched many times, greedily seeking technical knowledge.

そうして、ドイツに渡った男の一人に……
And so to one of the men who went to Germany: ......

小野派一刀流一六代宗家、笹木純蔵がいたのだ。
Junzo Sasagi, the 16th headmaster of the Ono-ha Itto-ryu school, was there.

彼はふとした事から知り合ったインメルマン少年に、一刀流剣術を手解きし、その才の尋常ならざるを知るや、奥義の伝授まで行った。……軽々しいというか、気前が良いというか、いささか変人だったようである。
In the event you have any questions regarding where by and how to use it, you can contact us at our own web site. This is a great way to make sure that you get the most out of your time and money.

だが彼は帰国の後、国粋の文化を売ったとしてこの行為に批判を浴びると、こう応えて一蹴した。　――学ぶのみで教えぬ者は、即ち知恵の盗人である。自分はドイツ軍に学び、返礼として少年に教えたのだ。
However, when he returned to Japan and was criticized for this act of selling nationalistic culture, he kicked it off with this response　--But when he returned to Japan and was criticized for selling nationalistic culture, he replied, "He who learns but does not teach is a thief of wisdom. I learned from the Germans, and I taught the boy in return.

かくしてインメルマンは一刀流の秘奥を拝受したのだが、教えた笹木にして彼がその秘技を活用できるだろうとまでは考えていなかったに違いない。
In this way, Immelmann received the secret of Itto-ryu, but Sasagi, who taught him, must not have thought that he would be able to use it.

一刀流五箇の秘伝は絶えず伝えられてきてこそいたものの、余りの難解さに使い得た者は始祖以来ついになく、技術ではなく単なる知識になり果てていた。　免許皆伝を示す一種の形式に過ぎなかったのである。
Although the five secrets of the Itto-Ryu had been passed down through the generations, they were so difficult to understand that no one had mastered them since their inception.　They were merely a formality to show that one had been granted the license.

だが、北仏戦線の極限状況にあって――　敵の剛強な騎士に追われたマックス・インメルマンは、差し迫る死に抗う渦中で遂に、秘剣の一つを蘇生させるに至ったのだ。
However, in the extreme conditions of the Northern French front, Max Immelmann, pursued by the enemy's powerful crafters, finally revives one of his secret swords in the midst of fighting against imminent death.

金翅鳥王剣。　垂直騎航からの反転落下攻撃。　自己より圧倒的に優る敵を討つ、起死回生の剣。
Golden-winged King Sword.　This is a reverse fall attack from a vertical craft.　A sword of resurrection to defeat an enemy who is far superior to you.

以後、インメルマンは常にこの技と共にあり、幾多の騎士を空から墜として敵味方を瞠目させた。　彼と彼の技は同一視され、その名は欧州を席巻し、悪魔的な恐怖と戦神的な畏怖の的となった。

戦場経験を有する署長は即座に知る。　軍だ。
The Chief, with his battlefield experience, knows immediately.　It's the military.

それも何らかの理由で統制を失い、完全な暴走状態に陥った小規模の軍部隊。　殺し壊し犯す餓狼の群れ。
It is a small military unit that has lost control for some reason and has gone completely berserk.　A pack of starving wolves who kill and destroy.

小規模といってもその戦力は、片瀬の一帯を焦土と化して余りあるであろう。　その前菜に軽武装の警官隊を蹴散らすことも容易かろう。
Even on a small scale, their strength would be enough to turn the whole area of Katase into a scorched earth.　It would be easy to kick out the lightly armed police force as an appetizer.

「あいつか……」
It's him or .......

その代名詞を、署長は呻いた。　　――銀星号。
The chief grunted at the pronoun.　　-- Silver Star.

景明を送り込んだ江ノ島で、何がどう推移したのかはわからない。　だがどうやら最後には当たりを引いたようだ。
I don't know what went on at Enoshima, where we sent Kageaki.　But apparently, he hit the bull's-eye in the end.

銀星号は顕現し……　そして、島にいた軍部隊を狂わせたのだろう。

--This time, it was a trap set by GHQ.　The Chief saw it that way, but he did not assume that Silver Star would never appear.

かくあるも考慮の内ではあった。　が、何が起ころうと島の中の事で済む――と、そう踏んでいたのだ。

市民に害が及ぶことはなかろうと。　……甘かった。

There was no way we could have predicted that Enoshima and Katase Beach would be adjacent to each other, but we had to consider the possibility that such a madness could upend the situation.

幾度も景明の報告を聞き、銀星号の尋常ならざるを彼に次ぐほどに知る身であったのだから！　拳が悔恨に震える。しかしもう遅い。
He had heard Kageaki's reports many times, and was second only to him in the knowledge of Silver Star's uncommonness!　My fists trembled with regret. But it was too late.

署長は見た。　背後でざわめき。彼の部下らも見たのだろう。
The chief saw it.　There was a buzz behind him. His men must have seen it, too.

黒々とした、人と車と肉と鉄の渦。　不揃いに吠え、ばらばらに駆け、だが一塊となって突き進む。
A black vortex of people, cars, flesh, and steel.　They barked unevenly, ran in disarray, but pushed forward as one.

あたかも祝福の戦車。　人々を踏み殺して極楽へ送る神の輿のように、殺戮を喜び踊りながら、それは片瀬へ向かって来る。
It was as if it was a blessed chariot.　Like a divine palanquin that tramples people to death and sends them to paradise, it comes toward Katase, rejoicing and dancing in the carnage.

署長は部下に迎撃隊形を指示した。　その効果の程を理解しながら。
The chief instructed his men to form an intercepting formation.　While understanding the extent of its effectiveness.

どう足掻こうと、防ぎ止めることはできない。　おそらく、千の死者を九百に減らすくらいが限度。
No matter how hard we try, we can't stop it.　Probably the limit is to reduce the death toll from a thousand to nine hundred.

焼け石に水だ。　しかし液体窒素の備えを怠ったのは彼だった。
It's not a good idea.　But it was he who had neglected to prepare the liquid nitrogen.
